* The person who smokes Pall Mall keeps a Bird, and since the Bird-keeper can't live in the same house as the Dog-keeper, they must live in different houses. Since the Bird-keeper is not yet assigned, we'll come back to them later.
* The owner of the Yellow house smokes Dunhill, so the Norwegian smokes Dunhill.
* The man who smokes Blends is neighbor of the one who keeps a Cat. Since the Cat-keeper isn't yet assigned, we'll come back to them later.
* The man who keeps a Horse lives next to the man who smokes Dunhill, so the Horse-keeper lives in the White house.

* The Norwegian lives next to the Blue house, so the Norwegian lives in the Yellow house.

	+ The Bird-keeper must live in the White house, as the Bird-keeper is not yet assigned and the House-keeper hasn't been assigned twice.
